They take an <a href="https://www.quantconnect.com/lean/docs#topic24450.html" target="_BLANK" class="lean-documentation" title="Open OrderEvent API Documentation">OrderEvent </a> , <a href="https://www.quantconnect.com/lean/docs#topic445.html" target="_BLANK" class="lean-documentation" title="Open Security API Documentation">Security </a> and <a href="https://www.quantconnect.com/lean/docs#topic26108.html" target="_BLANK" class="lean-documentation" title="Open SecurityPortfolioManager API Documentation">SecurityPortfolioManager </a> object and update the holdings to reflect the new final position. You should only need to update your portfolio model when you are create a new asset type. </p> 
          <p> Portfolio models implement the <a href="https://www.quantconnect.com/lean/docs#topic25341.html" target="_BLANK" class="lean-documentation" title="Open ISecurityPortfolioModel API Documentation">ISecurityPortfolioModel </a> interface. </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Reality-Modelling-Volatility-Model"> Volatility Model <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/02 Algorithm Reference/12 Reality Modelling/09 Volatility Model" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Reality-Modelling-Volatility-Model" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <p> The volatility model is a property of a security. Exactly how volatility is calculated varies a lot between strategies so we've provided an override point here. Volatility models get updated with data each time step and are expected to be updated immediately. This is primarily require for options backtesting. </p> 
          <p> Volatility models implement the <a href="https://www.quantconnect.com/lean/docs#topic25365.html" target="_BLANK" class="lean-documentation" title="Open IVolatilityModel API Documentation">IVolatilityModel </a> interface. We default to the NullVolatilityModel which returns 0 volatility at all times. As a helper we also provide the <a href="https://www.quantconnect.com/lean/docs#topic25845.html" target="_BLANK" class="lean-documentation" title="Open RelativeStandardDeviationVolatilityModel API Documentation">RelativeStandardDeviationVolatilityModel </a> which calculates the volatility based on standard deviation. </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="Charting"> Charting <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/02 Algorithm Reference/13 Charting" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Charting" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style=""> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Charting-Introduction-to-Charting"> Introduction to Charting <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/02 Algorithm Reference/13 Charting/01 Introduction to Charting" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Charting-Introduction-to-Charting" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <p> We provide a powerful charting API which can be build many chart types. At its simplest it can be used with a single line of code:</p>
          <pre class="csharp">Plot("Series Name", value);</pre>
          <pre class="python">Plot("Series Name", value)</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> With this code a line-graph is added underneath your <i>Strategy Equity</i> chart and your requested values are displayed over time. To create a new chart (new tab) you should also specify the chart name in your request:</p>
          <pre class="csharp">Plot("My Indicators", "EMA", ema);</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> Behind the scenes these methods create a new <a href="https://www.quantconnect.com/lean/docs#topic6940.html" target="_BLANK" class="lean-documentation" title="Open Chart API Documentation">Chart </a> object and add it to your algorithm, and then add a new <a href="https://www.quantconnect.com/lean/docs#topic6953.html" target="_BLANK" class="lean-documentation" title="Open Series API Documentation">Series </a> object to that chart. A chart is made from many series. You can also initialize your charts manually to get more control over their look and feel. </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style=""> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Charting-Manually-Creating-Charts"> Manually Creating Charts <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/02 Algorithm Reference/13 Charting/02 Manually Creating Charts" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Charting-Manually-Creating-Charts" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <p> In your initialize method you can use the <code>AddChart(Chart obj)</code> method to insert a new chart. Each chart object has an internal collection of Series objects. </p> 
          <p> In creating Series objects you must specify the name of the series, the <a href="https://www.quantconnect.com/lean/docs#topic6953.html" target="_BLANK" class="lean-documentation" title="Open SeriesType API Documentation">SeriesType </a> and the <i>index</i> the series operates on. The series index refers to its position in the chart - for example; if all the series are index 0, they will lay on top of each other. If each series has its own index, it will be have several mini-charts stack next to each other. </p> 
          <p> The picture below shows an EMA cross chart with both EMA series set to the same index: <img src="/i/docs/charting-overlay.png" class="img-responsive" data-pagespeed-url-hash="4177179645" onload="pagespeed.CriticalImages.checkImageForCriticality(this);"> Using different indexes the chart looks as follows: <img src="/i/docs/charting-stacked.png" class="img-responsive" data-pagespeed-url-hash="1378029056" onload="pagespeed.CriticalImages.checkImageForCriticality(this);"> </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">// In your initialize method:

// Chart - Master Container for the Chart:
var stockPlot = new Chart("Trade Plot");
// On the Trade Plotter Chart we want 3 series: trades and price:
var buyOrders = new Series("Buy", SeriesType.Scatter, 0);
var sellOrders = new Series("Sell", SeriesType.Scatter, 0);
var assetPrice = new Series("Price", SeriesType.Line, 0);
stockPlot.AddSeries(buyOrders);
stockPlot.AddSeries(sellOrders);
stockPlot.AddSeries(assetPrice);
AddChart(stockPlot);

// Later in your OnData(Slice data):
Plot("Trade Plot", "Price", data.Bars["SPY"].Close);</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python"># In your initialize method:
# Note - use single quotation marks: ' instead of double "
# Chart - Master Container for the Chart:
stockPlot = Chart('Trade Plot')
# On the Trade Plotter Chart we want 3 series: trades and price:
stockPlot.AddSeries(Series('Buy', SeriesType.Scatter, 0))
stockPlot.AddSeries(Series('Sell', SeriesType.Scatter, 0))
stockPlot.AddSeries(Series('Price', SeriesType.Line, 0))
self.AddChart(stockPlot)

// Later in your OnData(self, data):
self.Plot('Trade Plot', 'Price', self.lastPrice)</pre> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style=""> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Charting-Supported-Series-Types"> Supported Series Types <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/02 Algorithm Reference/13 Charting/03 Supported Series Types" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Charting-Supported-Series-Types" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <p> The charting API supports the follow series types. Nothing special is required to use these series, simply specify them for your series when creating your chart.</p>
          <pre>
   SeriesType.Line
             .Scatter
             .Candle
             .Bar
             .Flag
</pre> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Charting-Charting-Limitations"> Charting Limitations <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/02 Algorithm Reference/13 Charting/04 Charting Limitations" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Charting-Charting-Limitations" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <p> Intensive charting generates hundreds of megabytes (200MB) of data which is far too much to stream online or display in a web browser. Because of this we limit the number of points a chart can have to 4000. If you see an error <code>Exceeded maximum points per chart, data skipped</code> you have hit this limit and should reduce your sampling frequency. </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="Logging-and-Debug"> Logging and Debug <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/02 Algorithm Reference/14 Logging and Debug" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Logging-and-Debug" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style=""> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Logging-and-Debug-Debug-Messages"> Debug Messages <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/02 Algorithm Reference/14 Logging and Debug/01 Debug Messages" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Logging-and-Debug-Debug-Messages" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <meta name="tag" content="debugging and logging"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="debugging"> 
          <p> Algorithms can send debug messages to the console using the <code>Debug(string message)</code> method. Debug messages are capped at 200 characters long. If multiple identical messages are sent within 1 second we rate limit the messages to avoid crashing your browser. </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">Debug(Time.ToString("o") + " Purchasing AAPL: " + data["AAPL"].Price);</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python">self.Debug(str(self.Time) + " Purchasing AAPL: " + str(slice["SPY"].Price))</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example fsharp"> 
          <pre class="fsharp">this.Debug("Hello from FSharp")</pre> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style=""> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Logging-and-Debug-Errors-Messages"> Errors Messages <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/02 Algorithm Reference/14 Logging and Debug/02 Errors Messages" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Logging-and-Debug-Errors-Messages" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <p> Algorithms can send error messages to the console using the <code>Error(string message)</code> method. Error messages appear red in the console so you can see them easily. Like debug messages, error messages are rate limited to avoid flooding your browser. </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">Error("Volatility too high, terminating algorithm.");
Quit(); //Option: Instruct algorithm to stop.</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python">self.Error("Volatility too high, terminating algorithm.")
self.Quit() # Optional: Instruct algorithm to stop.</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example fsharp"> 
          <pre class="fsharp">this.Error("Volatility too high, triggering exit")
this.Quit()</pre> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Logging-and-Debug-Logging"> Logging <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/02 Algorithm Reference/14 Logging and Debug/03 Logging" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Logging-and-Debug-Logging" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <meta name="tag" content="debugging and logging"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="logging"> 
          <p> Algorithms can save more detailed messaging to log files for later analysis using <code>Log(string message)</code>. At the end of the backtest a link will be presented to view your results. In live trading a log viewer lets you view log results while the algorithm is running. Because of data vendor limitations price information cannot be recorded in logs. </p> 
          <p> Because of vendor limitations free users are capped to 10kb of logs per backtest, with a maximum of 3Mb per day. Users with a subscription can generate up to 100kb of logs per backtest. </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">Log("Additional detailed logging messages");</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python">self.Log("Additional detailed logging messages")</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example fsharp"> 
          <pre class="fsharp">this.Log("Additional detailed logging messages")</pre> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <h1>Asset Classes</h1> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="Equities"> Equities <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/03 Asset Classes/01 Equities" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Equities" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Equities-Equities"> <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/03 Asset Classes/01 Equities/01 Equities" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Equities-Equities" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <meta name="tag" content="using data"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="assets"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="equity"> 
          <p> </p>
          <h5 style="font-weight: bold;"> Backtesting </h5> 
          <p> There are roughly 16,400 symbols of survivorship bias free, split and dividend adjusted US equities data from Jan 1998 to today provided by QuantQuote. US Equities data by default arrives in adjusted format. </p> 
          <p> Our data is provided by QuantQuote and is <b>trade</b> data only only with tick, second, minute, hour and daily resolutions available. </p> 
          <p> The Tick data is raw and unfiltered - which includes suspicious, untradable and off market ticks. This can often result in unrealistic backtests. Before using tick data you should fully understand all the exchange codes and the "suspicious" flag which indicates a tick you should ignore. Unless you're an expert you should use the pre-filtered second and minute data. </p> 
          <p> In backtesting QuantConnect tick data is ordered but rounded to the previous second. There is no millisecond timestamp on the data. </p> 
          <h5 style="font-weight: bold;"> Live Trading </h5> 
          <p> QuantConnect live tick data comes directly from the exchanges. Like backtesting tick data, it is also raw and unfiltered. </p> 
          <p> When deploying an algorithm to Interactive Brokers you also have the option to use them for your datafeed. When using Interactive Brokers for your datafeed you must make sure you're subscribed to the asset classes you need. </p> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Selecting Data </h3> Subscribe to equity data: 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>
// Complete Add Equity API - Including Default Parameters:
AddEquity(string ticker,
          Resolution resolution = Resolution.Minute,
          string market = Market.USA, 
          bool fillDataForward = true,
          decimal leverage = 0m,
          bool extendedMarketHours = false)
</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Using Data </h3> 
          <p> Trades can be accessed in the Slice or TradeBars object in OnData event handler: </p> 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>var bar = data["SPY"];</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> Other information about the equity can be found in the <a href="#Securities-and-Portfolio">security</a> object: </p> 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>var equity = Securities["SPY"];</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Live Trading </h3> Only available with Interactive Brokers. 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">// In Initialize
AddEquity("SPY", Resolution.Minute);</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python"># In Initialize
self.AddEquity("SPY", Resolution.Minute)</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">// In OnData(Slice data) or OnData(TradeBars data)
var bar = data["SPY"];

// Anywhere in the code
var equity = Securities["SPY"];</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python"># In OnData(self, data)
bar = data["SPY"]

# Anywhere in the code
equity = self.Securities["SPY"]</pre> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="Forex"> Forex <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/03 Asset Classes/02 Forex" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Forex" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Forex-Forex"> <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/03 Asset Classes/02 Forex/01 Forex" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Forex-Forex" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <meta name="tag" content="using data"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="assets"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="forex"> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Data Available </h3> 
          <p> 13 major currency pairs from Apr 2007 to now provided by FXCM and 71 major currency pairs from Apr 2004 to now provided by OANDA. </p> 
          <p> <b><u> Backtesting mode</u></b> </p> Quotes with tick, second, minute, hour and daily resolutions are available. 
          <p> <b><u> Live mode</u></b> </p> Tick data is available from FXCM and OANDA. 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Selecting Data </h3> Subscribe to forex data: 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>
// Complete Add Forex API - Including Default Parameters:
AddForex(string pair,
         Resolution resolution = Resolution.Minute,
         string market = null,
         bool fillDataForward = true,
         decimal leverage = 0m)
</pre> 
          <p></p> By default, FXCM is the data provider. If we want to use OANDA instead, we have to explicitly select it: 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>AddForex("EURUSD", Resolution.Minute, Market.Oanda);</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Accessing data </h3> 
          <p> Quotes can be accessed in the Slice or TradeBars object in OnData event handler: </p> 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>var bar = data["EURUSD"];</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> Other information about the forex pair can be found in the <a href="#Securities-and-Portfolio">security</a> object: </p> 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>var forex = Securities["EURUSD"];</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Live Trading </h3> Available with FXCM, OANDA and Interactive Brokers. 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">// In Initialize
AddForex("EURUSD", Resolution.Minute);   // or
AddForex("EURUSD", Resolution.Minute, Market.FXCM);

// For OANDA, we need to explictly define the market
AddForex("EURUSD", Resolution.Minute, Market.Oanda);</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python"># In Initialize
self.AddForex("EURUSD", Resolution.Minute)   # or
self.AddForex("EURUSD", Resolution.Minute, Market.FXCM)

# For OANDA, we need to explictly define the market
self.AddForex("EURUSD", Resolution.Minute, Market.Oanda)</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">// In OnData(Slice data) or OnData(QuoteBars data)
var bar = data["EURUSD"];

// Anywhere in the code
var forex = Securities["EURUSD"];</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python"># In OnData(self, data)
bar = data["EURUSD"]

# Anywhere in the code
equity = self.Securities["EURUSD"]</pre> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="Futures"> Futures <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/03 Asset Classes/03 Futures" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Futures" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Futures-Futures"> <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/03 Asset Classes/03 Futures/01 Futures" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Futures-Futures" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <meta name="tag" content="using data"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="assets"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="futures"> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Data Available </h3> 
          <p> <b><u> Backtesting mode</u></b> </p> 4000 symbols of futures contracts from Jan 2009 to now provided by AlgoSeek. 
          <p> Quotes and trades with tick, second, minute resolutions are available. </p> 
          <p> <b><u> Live mode</u></b> </p> 
          <p> Live tick data from Interactive Brokers are available. You MUST have a valid <a href="https://www.interactivebrokers.com/en/software/am/am/manageaccount/marketdatasubscriptions.htm">data subscription</a> with IB). </p> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Selecting Data </h3> Subscribe to futures data: 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>
// Complete Add Future API - Including Default Parameters:
AddFuture(string symbol,
          Resolution resolution = Resolution.Minute,
          string market = null,
          bool fillDataForward = true,
          decimal leverage = 0m)      
</pre> 
          <p></p> By default, the futures universe is filtered down to contracts that expire within 35 days. A difference set of contracts can be chosen with the 
          <code>SetFilter</code> method: 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>
var future = AddFuture(Futures.Indices.SP500EMini);
future.SetFilter(TimeSpan.FromDays(30), TimeSpan.FromDays(180));
</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> Quotes and trades can be accessed in the Slice object in OnData event handler. </p> 
          <p> The FuturesChains member contains a FutureChain object for each subscribed future: </p> 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>
// In Initialize
FutureSymbol = future.Symbol;

// In OnData
FuturesChain chain;
slice.FuturesChains.TryGetValue(FutureSymbol, out chain);
</pre> 
          <p></p> An FuturesChain object has information about the undelying and futures contracts that were filtered by 
          <code>SetFilter</code>: 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>
var underlying = chain.Underlying;
var contracts = chain.Contracts; 
</pre> 
          <p> Finally, we can use Linq to select the contract(s) we want to trade. </p>
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Live Trading </h3> Only available with Interactive Brokers. 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">// In Initialize
var future = AddFuture(Futures.Indices.SP500EMini, Resolution.Minute);
future.SetFilter(TimeSpan.Zero, TimeSpan.FromDays(182));</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python"># In Initialize
future = self.AddFuture(Futures.Indices.SP500EMini, Resolution.Minute)
futureSetFilter(timedelta(0), timedelta(182))</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">// In Initialize
FutureSymbol = future.Symbol;

// In OnData(Slice slice)
FuturesChain chain;
if (slice.FuturesChains.TryGetValue(FutureSymbol, out chain))
{
    var underlying = chain.Underlying;
    var contracts = chain.Contracts.Value; 
    foreach (var contract in contracts)
    {
        //
    }
}</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python"># In Initialize
self.FutureSymbol = future.Symbol;

// In OnData(self, slice)
chain = slice.FuturesChains[self.FutureSymbol]
underlying = chain.Underlying
contracts = chain.Contracts.Value
for contract in contracts:
    pass</pre> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="Options"> Options <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/03 Asset Classes/04 Options" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Options" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Options-Options"> <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/03 Asset Classes/04 Options/01 Options" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Options-Options" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <meta name="tag" content="using data"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="assets"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="options"> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Data Available </h3> 
          <p> <b><u> Backtesting mode</u></b> </p> 4000 symbols of US equity options from Jan 2010 to now provided by AlgoSeek. 
          <p></p> Quotes and trades with minute resolution only. 
          <p> <b><u> Live mode</u></b> </p> 
          <p> Live tick data from Interactive Brokers are available. You MUST have a valid <a href="https://www.interactivebrokers.com/en/software/am/am/manageaccount/marketdatasubscriptions.htm">data subscription</a> with IB). </p> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Selecting Data </h3> Subscribe to options data: 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>
// Complete Add Option API - Including Default Parameters:
AddOption(string underlying,
          Resolution resolution = Resolution.Minute,
          string market = null,
          bool fillDataForward = true,
          decimal leverage = 0m)
</pre> 
          <p></p> By default, the option universe is filtered down to contracts that expire within 35 days, one contract below and another above ATM, and exclude weeklys. A difference set of contracts can be chosen with the 
          <code>SetFilter</code> method: 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>
var option = AddOption("GOOG");
option.SetFilter(-2, 2, TimeSpan.FromDays(30), TimeSpan.FromDays(180));
</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <code>SetFilter</code> also accepts Linq expressions and enables the section of weeklys and define the desired option right: 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>
var option = AddOption("GOOG");
option.SetFilter(universe =&gt;
		 from symbol in universe                                .WeeklysOnly()                                .Expiration(TimeSpan.Zero, TimeSpan.FromDays(10))                                    where symbol.ID.OptionRight != OptionRight.Put &amp;&amp;                                    universe.Underlying.Price - symbol.ID.StrikePrice 
	&lt; 60
                                    select symbol);
</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Accessing data </h3> Quotes and trades can be accessed in the Slice object in OnData event handler. 
          <br> The OptionChains member contains an OptionChain object for each subscribed option: 
          <br> 
          <pre>
// In Initialize
OptionSymol = option.Symbol;

// In OnData
OptionChain chain;
slice.OptionChains.TryGetValue(OptionSymbol, out chain);
</pre> 
          <br> An OptionChain object has information about the undelying and options contracts that were filtered by 
          <code>SetFilter</code>: 
          <br> 
          <pre>
var underlying = chain.Underlying;
var contracts = chain.Contracts; 
</pre> 
          <br> Finally, we can use Linq to select the contract(s) we want to trade. 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Live Trading </h3> Only available with Interactive Brokers. 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">// In Initialize
var option = AddOption("GOOG");
option.SetFilter(-2, 2, TimeSpan.Zero, TimeSpan.FromDays(182));
// or Linq
option.SetFilter(universe =&gt; from symbol in universe
                                .WeeklysOnly()
                                .Expiration(TimeSpan.Zero, TimeSpan.FromDays(10))
                                    where symbol.ID.OptionRight != OptionRight.Put &amp;&amp;
                                    universe.Underlying.Price - symbol.ID.StrikePrice &lt; 60
                                    select symbol);</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python"># In Initialize
option = self.AddOption("GOOG");
option.SetFilter(-2, 2, timedelta(0), timedelta(182))</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">// In Initialize
OptionSymol = option.Symbol;

// In OnData
OptionChain chain;
if (slice.OptionChains.TryGetValue(OptionSymbol, out chain))
{
    // we find at the money (ATM) put contract with farthest expiration
    var atmContract = chain
        .OrderByDescending(x =&gt; x.Expiry)
        .ThenBy(x =&gt; Math.Abs(chain.Underlying.Price - x.Strike))
        .ThenByDescending(x =&gt; x.Right)
        .FirstOrDefault();
}</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python"># In Initialize
self.OptionSymol = option.Symbol;

// In OnData
chain = slice.OptionChains[self.OptionSymbol].Value
# we sort the contracts to find at the money (ATM) contract with farthest expiration
contracts = sorted(sorted(chain, \
    key = lambda x: abs(chain.Underlying.Price - x.Strike)), \
    key = lambda x: x.Expiry, reverse=True)</pre> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="CFD"> CFD <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/03 Asset Classes/05 CFD" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#CFD" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="CFD-CFD"> <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/03 Asset Classes/05 CFD/01 CFD" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#CFD-CFD" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <meta name="tag" content="using data"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="assets"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="cfd"> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Data Available </h3> 50 contracts from Apr 2004 to now provided by OANDA. 
          <p> <b><u> Backtesting mode</u></b> </p> Quotes with tick, second, minute, hour and daily resolutions are available. 
          <p> <b><u> Live mode</u></b> </p> Tick data is available from OANDA. 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Selecting Data </h3> Subscribe to forex data: 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>
// Complete Add CFD API - Including Default Parameters:
AddCfd(string ticker,
       Resolution resolution = Resolution.Minute,
       string market = null,
       bool fillDataForward = true,
       decimal leverage = 0m)
</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Accessing data </h3> Quotes can be accessed in the Slice or TradeBars object in OnData event handler: 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>var bar = data["XAUUSD"];</pre> 
          <p></p> Other information about the contract can be found in the 
          <a href="#Securities-and-Portfolio">security</a> object: 
          <p> </p>
          <pre>var cfd = Securities["XAUUSD"];</pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h3> Live Trading </h3> Only available with OANDA. 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">// In Initialize
AddCfd("XAUUSD", Resolution.Minute, Market.Oanda);</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python"># In Initialize
self.AddCfd("XAUUSD", Resolution.Minute. Market.Oanda)</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">// In OnData(Slice data) or OnData(QuoteBars data)
var bar = data["XAUUSD"];

// Anywhere in the code
var cfd = Securities["XAUUSD"];</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python">// In OnData(self, data)
bar = data["XAUUSD"];

// Anywhere in the code
cfd = self.Securities["XAUUSD"]</pre> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <h1>Live Trading</h1> 
       <div class="row section">

         <h2 id="Supported-Brokerages"> Supported Brokerages <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/04 Live Trading/01 Supported Brokerages" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Supported-Brokerages" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2>

          <meta name="tag" content="live trading"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="brokerage support">

Algorithms can be deployed immediately at any time of the day or night. A subscription is required for live trading however many brokerages sponsor live trading for their clients. </p>

         <h2 id="Notifications"> Notifications <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/04 Live Trading/02 Notifications" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Notifications" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2>

       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Notifications-Notifications"> <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/04 Live Trading/02 Notifications/01 Notifications" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Notifications-Notifications" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <meta name="tag" content="live trading"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="alerts"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="email"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="sms"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="web-hook"> 
          <p> In live trading mode we allow sending Email, SMS and Web-Hook notifications to notify you of significant events. You can send up to <b>20</b> notifications per hour. <b>These are only sent during live trading.</b> </p> 
          <p> </p>
          <table class="table table-striped"> 
           <thead> 
            <tr> 
             <th style="width: 150px;"> Method </th> 
             <th> Code Snippet </th> 
            </tr> 
           </thead> 
           <tbody> 
            <tr> 
             <td class="notify"> <i class="fa fa-phone"></i> SMS </td> 
             <td> <code>Notify.Sms(string phoneNumber, string message);</code> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td class="notify"> <i class="fa fa-envelope-o"></i> Email </td> 
             <td> <code>Notify.Email(string address, string subject, string message, string data = "");</code> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td class="notify"> <i class="fa fa-external-link"></i> Web Hook </td> 
             <td> <code>Notify.Web(string address, object data = null);</code> </td> 
            </tr> 
           </tbody> 
          </table> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">//Send yourself an email on live trade executions
Notify.Email("myEmailAddress@gmail.com", "Live Trade Executed", "Bought 100 Shares of AAPL");</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python">#Send yourself an email on live trade executions

         <h2 id="Runtime-Statistics"> Runtime Statistics <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/04 Live Trading/03 Runtime Statistics" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Runtime-Statistics" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Runtime-Statistics-Runtime-Statistics"> <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/04 Live Trading/03 Runtime Statistics/01 Runtime Statistics" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Runtime-Statistics-Runtime-Statistics" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <meta name="tag" content="live trading"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="runtime statistics"> 
          <p> Runtime statistics are custom defined banner statistics displayed across the top of your live algorithm. </p> 
          <img class="img-responsive" src="/i/docs/docs-live-runtime.png" data-pagespeed-url-hash="2253123801" onload="pagespeed.CriticalImages.checkImageForCriticality(this);"> 
          <p> You can add your own runtime-statistics using the <code>SetRuntimeStatistic(string name, string value);</code> method. In the image above the user displays the current value of BTC: <code>SetRuntimeStatistic("BTC", data["BTC"].Close);</code> </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
         <div class="section-example csharp"> 
          <pre class="csharp">// User displays the current value of BTC
SetRuntimeStatistic("BTC", data["BTC"].Close);</pre> 
         </div> 
         <div class="section-example python"> 
          <pre class="python"># User displays the current value of BTC
btc = self.Securities["BTC"].Symbol
self.SetRuntimeStatistic("BTC", data[btc].Close)</pre> 
         </div>

       <h1>Research</h1> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="Introduction-to-Jupyter"> Introduction to Jupyter <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/05 Research/01 Introduction to Jupyter" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Introduction-to-Jupyter" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Introduction-to-Jupyter-Introduction"> Introduction <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/05 Research/01 Introduction to Jupyter/01 Introduction" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Introduction-to-Jupyter-Introduction" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <meta name="tag" content="research"> 
          <meta name="tag" content="quantbook"> 
          <p> QuantConnect provides an environment for you to perform exploratory research and brainstorm new ideas for algorithm. We simply call this the <a target="_BLANK" href="/research">research</a> environment. Here you can run Python CLI commands and explore the data directly from a <a target="_BLANK" href="http://jupyter.org/">Jupyter notebook</a> installed in QuantConnect. </p> 
          <p> Inside a notebook you can perform virtually any command inside a safe disposable environment. We automatically save your notebook for you. Currently we just support Python 2.7 notebooks. </p> 
          <p> You can share a notebook by clicking the <i class="fa fa-sharing"></i> icon in the bottom right of the page. You can also share a notebook directly to the forums when you create a new discussion or comment. </p> 
          <p> The foundational class for access QuantConnect data in Jupyter is the <code>QuantBook</code>. This is a wrapper on the QCAlgorithm class and has many of the same methods. The research environment is currently in beta but we are slowly adding new methods to the QuantBook to expand your research potential. The basic template provides the foundation code required to import the QuantBook class. Specifically: </p> 
          <pre class="prettyprint">
from clr import AddReference
AddReference("System")
AddReference("QuantConnect.Common")
AddReference("QuantConnect.Jupyter")
AddReference("QuantConnect.Indicators")
from System import *
from QuantConnect import *
from QuantConnect.Data.Market import TradeBar, QuoteBar
from QuantConnect.Jupyter import *
from QuantConnect.Indicators import *
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import pandas as pd

# Create an instance
qb = QuantBook()
</pre> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="Historical-Data"> Historical Data <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/05 Research/02 Historical Data" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Historical-Data" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Historical-Data-Historical-Data"> <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/05 Research/02 Historical Data/01 Historical Data" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Historical-Data-Historical-Data" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="Using-Indicators"> Using Indicators <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/05 Research/03 Using Indicators" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Using-Indicators" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy">

       <h1>Other</h1> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="Frequently-Asked-Questions"> Frequently Asked Questions <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/06 Other/01 Frequently Asked Questions" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Frequently-Asked-Questions" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Frequently-Asked-Questions-Frequently-Asked-Questions"> <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/06 Other/01 Frequently Asked Questions/01 Frequently Asked Questions" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Frequently-Asked-Questions-Frequently-Asked-Questions" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <p> For a full list of Frequently Asked Questions please see the <a href="https://www.quantconnect.com/faq" target="_BLANK">FAQ</a> page. </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="Common-Errors"> Common Errors <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/06 Other/02 Common Errors" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Common-Errors" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Common-Errors-Common-Errors"> <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/06 Other/02 Common Errors/01 Common Errors" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Common-Errors-Common-Errors" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <p> </p>
          <h4> Runtime Error: 'AAPL' wasn't found in the TradeBars object </h4> 
          <p> You're attempting to access data which is not in the TradeBars dictionary. There are two key reasons for this: <br> 1. You have not requested data for this security in the Initialize method. <br> 2. The data has gaps because it is not filling forward, or you're accessing the data after-hours when there won't be any price information. </p> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> </p>
          <h4> Backtest Error: Error initializing algorithm: Date Invalid </h4> 
          <p> You may have accidentally put invalid start and end dates into your algorithm. Or potentially you pressed backtest before the algorithm was fully saved. Please Ctrl+S to save the document, wait for its confirmation, and then click Backtest again. </p> 
          <p></p> 
          <p> &nbsp; </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section"> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12"> 
         <h2 id="Coding-Environment"> Coding Environment <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/06 Other/03 Coding Environment" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true" style="font-size:0.7em;"></i> </a> <a href="#Coding-Environment" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h2> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container"></div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style=""> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy"> 
          <h3 id="Coding-Environment-Local-Development"> Local Development <a href="https://github.com/QuantConnect/Documentation/tree/master/06 Other/03 Coding Environment/01 Local Development" class="anchor-link" target="_blank"> <i class="fa fa-github" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> <a href="#Coding-Environment-Local-Development" class="anchor-link"> <i class="fa fa-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></i> </a> </h3> 
          <p> We recommend using <a href="https://www.visualstudio.com/downloads/" target="_BLANK">Visual Studio Community Edition</a> as your programming environment. The community edition has the full power of Visual Studio and enables programming in C#, F#, VB and Python. If you're running on Mac or Linux you can also use <a href="http://www.monodevelop.com/download/" target="_BLANK">MonoDevelop</a> or <a href="https://www.visualstudio.com/vs/visual-studio-mac/" target="_BLANK">Xamarin Studio</a>. </p> 
          <p> If you prefer coding locally, you can run LEAN inside Visual Studio. The LEAN installation takes about 5 minutes and allows you to backtest locally and copy-paste your algorithms into QuantConnect.com. Check out the <a href="https://lean.quantconnect.com/docs#topic14.html" target="_BLANK">LEAN-Getting Started Tutorial</a> for more information. </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-example-container section-fill"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="section-background"></div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row section" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #eee; "> 
        <div class="col-lg-6 col-md-6 col-sm-12 section-copy-container"> 
         <div class="section-copy">
